  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

      initializeSiwa();

      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer18291715437429470511">This book is Out-of-Print.<br/><br/>"One man's search for a mystery author catapults him into a dangerous race to unlock esoteric wisdom that has been hidden and disputed for thousands of years"<br/> Peter Ashton has a dark past. In a teenage prank he uses an old book to perform an occult ritual. The experiment goes awry and his best friend is killed in the act.<br/> Two decades later Peter t</span>
  <span id="freeText18291715437429470511" style="display:none">This book is Out-of-Print.<br /><br />"One man's search for a mystery author catapults him into a dangerous race to unlock esoteric wisdom that has been hidden and disputed for thousands of years"<br /> Peter Ashton has a dark past. In a teenage prank he uses an old book to perform an occult ritual. The experiment goes awry and his best friend is killed in the act.<br /> Two decades later Peter travels to Europe to discover the secrets of the book and its mystery author. Plagued by curiosity and guilt he meets a Professor and an English Auctioneer who try to help him verify its authenticity and origins. The result is far beyond what he imagined. It is the last unpublished secret work by 19th century French occultist Eliphas Levi. The book’s meaning is shrouded in mystical conspiracy like its author. Peter soon finds it brings unwanted attention.<br /> Bonnet was once a dedicated American government agent but is descending on a dark mystical path. He uses an occult tool to enhance his abilities but at a grave personal cost. He desires occult power and is killing everyone that stands in the way. Will he catch Peter and his priceless book?<br /> From Paris to Los Angeles Peter races against time and powerful enemies. A cult leader opens his eyes to the extent of underground mysticism and tempts him with money and power. With limited options Peter is attacked by extremists desperate to get hold of the book. A beautiful gypsy woman gives him hope and insight. The final clue leads him to a Spanish mansion with more revelations than he dreamed possible.<br /> Can Peter unlock the secret wisdom before it is too late? Or will he be seduced by the deadly forces that tempted him 20 years ago….</span>
  <a data-text-id="18291715437429470511" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_907226293" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/907226293" />
    <a title="Ryan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30454385-ryan"><img alt="Ryan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1397432860p2/30454385.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/907226293?book_show_action=true">Apr 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ryan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ryan" href="/user/show/30454385-ryan">Ryan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer907226293" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5467562473773344844"><br/>Once I finished the prologue of Simon W. Clark's thriller The Book of Occult, I was immediately hooked. There is something about the way this author strings his words together that is evocative, real, and utterly captivating. I did most of my reading for the book on my way to and from work on the train, and every single time, I never wanted to get out!<br/><br/>There is quite a wide variety of different genres in this book. I felt that every chapter had something new to offer me, so I would never get bore</span>
  <span id="freeText5467562473773344844" style="display:none"><br />Once I finished the prologue of Simon W. Clark's thriller The Book of Occult, I was immediately hooked. There is something about the way this author strings his words together that is evocative, real, and utterly captivating. I did most of my reading for the book on my way to and from work on the train, and every single time, I never wanted to get out!<br /><br />There is quite a wide variety of different genres in this book. I felt that every chapter had something new to offer me, so I would never get bored; there are nearly sixty chapters in all. That is a lot of chapters, so this is a telling aspect of the author's ability to craft an excellent, fast-moving narrative. The settings are constantly changing too -- Peter's quest to search for the author of the titular book brings him all across the world. Yet despite this long journey, the author allows us the necessary breaks and rises in tension to keep us gripping our seats the whole way while giving us time to breathe.<br /><br />Most of all, the plot in this book is fantastic. It isn't too over the top, and while calling it believable in our world might be a bit of a stretch, the writing is top notch and it kept me excited all the way through. I am truly hoping for a sequel!</span>
  <a data-text-id="5467562473773344844" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_892796737" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/892796737" />
    <a title="Michele" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30018648-michele"><img alt="Michele" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1395963131p2/30018648.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/892796737?book_show_action=true">Mar 26, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michele" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michele" href="/user/show/30018648-michele">Michele</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer892796737" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5432964782242795147">While I am someone that doesn't often read books like this, I found it all very interested. Clark's writing style kept things interesting, and his knowledge of the subject was wonderful, as it made the story much easier to believe. I am now compelled to read more books of this genre, and am excited to see what more he writes in the future.<br/>Alternating between two very different men looking for similar answers, this story stayed interesting from start to finish. While Bonnet was not favorable, it </span>
  <span id="freeText5432964782242795147" style="display:none">While I am someone that doesn't often read books like this, I found it all very interested. Clark's writing style kept things interesting, and his knowledge of the subject was wonderful, as it made the story much easier to believe. I am now compelled to read more books of this genre, and am excited to see what more he writes in the future.<br />Alternating between two very different men looking for similar answers, this story stayed interesting from start to finish. While Bonnet was not favorable, it was his tragedy that made me want to continue reading, and I wanted to discover how everything turned out for him. The hope of Peter was a wonderful contradiction to Bonnet, and I continuously wondered how and if the two would meet.<br />I would recommend this to readers interested in thrillers and fantasy, but also to those looking for something new. I was pleasantly surprised by this story, and as I said before, I cannot wait to see what more Clark has in store.</span>

<div id="review_884544408" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/884544408" />
    <a title="Adam Mcprime" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/29742079-adam-mcprime"><img alt="Adam Mcprime" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1395103385p2/29742079.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/884544408?book_show_action=true">Mar 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Adam Mcprime" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Adam Mcprime" href="/user/show/29742079-adam-mcprime">Adam Mcprime</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">All who like the occult or a good story!</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer884544408" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16811758076393171351">As somebody who is always looking to read some new occult work, I can say that The Book of Occult never let me down. From the engaging prologue right to the end I thoroughly enjoyed the adventure told within. <br/><br/>Although I’m quite new to the niche itself, I never found myself too confused or felt out of the loop throughout. The story is told in a way so it does not exclude anybody from enjoying it – I could easily pass this to a friend who knows nothing of the occult who would enjoy this equally.<br/><br/>I </span>
  <span id="freeText16811758076393171351" style="display:none">As somebody who is always looking to read some new occult work, I can say that The Book of Occult never let me down. From the engaging prologue right to the end I thoroughly enjoyed the adventure told within. <br /><br />Although I’m quite new to the niche itself, I never found myself too confused or felt out of the loop throughout. The story is told in a way so it does not exclude anybody from enjoying it – I could easily pass this to a friend who knows nothing of the occult who would enjoy this equally.<br /><br />I did find that I picked up a lot of insightful knowledge on the occult throughout, too. I mainly picked it up due to a growing love for the occult but immediately found myself captured in the plot as well. Certainly worth a read on my own experience with the book – whether you just enjoy a good read, or are looking to explore an enjoyable niche. <br /><br />Aside from the plot, the style of writing is very easy to enjoy, too. I was surprised to find out that this was the first release from the writer as there are relatively little moments in the book that you could do a disservice. At the same time, it also does not give you a linear path of thought to follow – it opens up many different avenues with giving us the story from more than one perspective.<br /><br />Although some might not like that touch and style in books, or certain movies, it’s something I certainly enjoy. It keeps the pace nice and high, while still allowing for important character building backstory as well as time for learning new important parts about the occult culture as a whole. <br /><br />Overall, this is one that I’ll be reading again in the future and has given me a thirst for the genre. I’d like to try and learn more about the occult from various sources, and figured I’d be doing that mostly through online reading – it’s certainly more enjoyable with a plot though! </span>
  <a data-text-id="16811758076393171351" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_904835761" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/904835761" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30382681-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1397050983p2/30382681.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/904835761?book_show_action=true">Apr 08, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/30382681-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer904835761" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14690539157888428369">I'm a huge fan of suspense and thrilling books, and I was intrigued about the 'Occult' aspect of this book. I loved the quality in which the book was written and how well the author, Simon W. Clark, sets up the plot and characters from the very beginning. Even from the very first pages I was hooked into the book and eager to read more. Before this book I had not delved into occult or occult related subjects, but I found it to be extremely fascinating to be immersed into this fantastically imagin</span>
  <span id="freeText14690539157888428369" style="display:none">I'm a huge fan of suspense and thrilling books, and I was intrigued about the 'Occult' aspect of this book. I loved the quality in which the book was written and how well the author, Simon W. Clark, sets up the plot and characters from the very beginning. Even from the very first pages I was hooked into the book and eager to read more. Before this book I had not delved into occult or occult related subjects, but I found it to be extremely fascinating to be immersed into this fantastically imagined world. <br /><br />I was very pleased to find that the book was not slow, but was quite the opposite, always keeping a fast paced tempo without losing important storyline and details. The exciting storyline mixed with the interesting subject matter, makes it extremely difficult to put down this book. <br /><br />There is definitely a lot in the world that is considered 'unknown' and I think this aspect of the book makes it a lot more personal. While reading I could imagine myself in these situations or wonder if other people I know have ever been introduced into the occult. I even found myself thinking that it would definitely add a lot more excitement to my life to be a part of secret occult, but then again, it depends what the occult's beliefs were!<br /><br />Overall, I highly recommend this book to all types of readers, and encourage people to open their mind and allow the genius of “The Book of Occult” to be a fun escape into the 'unknown'.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14690539157888428369" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText7932977783461415214" style="display:none">History, suspense, and a phenomenal story line- Oh My! Every now and then I will find the diamond in the rough- a book that is right up my genre alley that is actually well written and compelling. Well here it is. <br /><br />After an unseeingly mishap with the workings of operating an occult ritual, a ready to be world traveler embarks on a journey to find any clues or answers to what could be one of the most mysterious findings to date. <br /><br />Without giving too much away, I must say the author knows how to capture his readers and make them beg for the main characters mercy. This novel will definitely be loved by many and I look forward to seeing more from this author in the future!<br /></span>

<div id="review_1039198832" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1039198832" />
    <a title="Abigail Van nuys" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33999314-abigail-van-nuys"><img alt="Abigail Van nuys" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1409594580p2/33999314.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1039198832?book_show_action=true">Aug 28, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Abigail Van nuys" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Abigail Van nuys" href="/user/show/33999314-abigail-van-nuys">Abigail Van nuys</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1039198832" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11788308073449354695">I won't write too much about the storyline as that can be found in the blurb and description on amazon anyway. This tale starts off plunging right into the action which I really like from a thriller. The next 100 pages or so have a plethora of different characters and mini-plots which seems to stream together by the middle of this tale. The main characters are aptly dealt with and their development is spasmodic especially the bad guy who I found rather full-on. The interaction and activity heats</span>
  <span id="freeText11788308073449354695" style="display:none">I won't write too much about the storyline as that can be found in the blurb and description on amazon anyway. This tale starts off plunging right into the action which I really like from a thriller. The next 100 pages or so have a plethora of different characters and mini-plots which seems to stream together by the middle of this tale. The main characters are aptly dealt with and their development is spasmodic especially the bad guy who I found rather full-on. The interaction and activity heats up even more in the second half. In closure I think the final moments are handled well and don't leave me wondering.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11788308073449354695" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText15544328127197153228" style="display:none">Once I read the prologue, I knew I was in for an action packed story.   <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/935923512" />
    <a title="Monica" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28889730-monica"><img alt="Monica" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1400096081p2/28889730.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/935923512?book_show_action=true">May 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Monica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Monica" href="/user/show/28889730-monica">Monica</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer935923512" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8707727430713389261">Seatbelt recommended – this is a wild ride!<br/><br/>Mr. Clark’s The Book of Occult was a fantastic read! For grown-up Harry Potter fans that wish there was a little more magic in Dan Brown’s transcontinental history thrillers, The Book of Occult is pure adventure from start to finish. This book has it all: endearing characters with interesting stories, history, antiquities, dark magic, politics, adventure and vivid descriptions of times and places. I was immediately drawn to Peter, an intriguing young ma</span>
  <span id="freeText8707727430713389261" style="display:none">Seatbelt recommended – this is a wild ride!<br /><br />Mr. Clark’s The Book of Occult was a fantastic read! For grown-up Harry Potter fans that wish there was a little more magic in Dan Brown’s transcontinental history thrillers, The Book of Occult is pure adventure from start to finish. This book has it all: endearing characters with interesting stories, history, antiquities, dark magic, politics, adventure and vivid descriptions of times and places. I was immediately drawn to Peter, an intriguing young man who tragically lost a friend in the riveting prologue, and cheered for him the rest of the book, watching to learn if something could be uncovered to answer the mystery of the manuscript he holds. The other story lines were plentiful and equally compelling and Mr. Clark did a superb job weaving them together into a masterpiece of a novel.<br /> <br />This book contained a moderate salting of a transgeographical-based plot, a smattering of commentary on the history of magic and its place in the modern day and a light icing of politics, world events and romance. All together, the layers of this delectable novel are utterly satisfying.<br /><br />Mr. Clark’s writing talents are superb and his style of storytelling is polished and captivating. Quite literally, I couldn’t put this book down and read voraciously in one sitting, anxious to know what twist or turn was going to send me into heart palpitations next. This is a book I thoroughly enjoyed and really I only have one regret: I reached the end and now it’s over. <br /><br />Well done, Mr. Clark. I look forward to reading more from your pen soon.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8707727430713389261" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer7984075912175033130">My friend recommended I read Simon W. Clark’s ‘The Book of Occult’ because she knows I love books about the occult. She likened it to 'The Da Vinci Code', which we both enjoyed. I was immediately hooked after reading the prologue. Peter's quest to find the meaning behind his childhood friends death leads him to Paris, years later, for answers. The book was perfectly paced and filled with action, intrigue, and suspense. Even better, the author was able to come up with a perfect ending to his stor</span>
  <span id="freeText7984075912175033130" style="display:none">My friend recommended I read Simon W. Clark’s ‘The Book of Occult’ because she knows I love books about the occult. She likened it to 'The Da Vinci Code', which we both enjoyed. I was immediately hooked after reading the prologue. Peter's quest to find the meaning behind his childhood friends death leads him to Paris, years later, for answers. The book was perfectly paced and filled with action, intrigue, and suspense. Even better, the author was able to come up with a perfect ending to his story, which so rarely happens.<br /><br />The Book of Occult takes you from country to country trying to unravel the secrets of the occult. The settings, along with the characters, were all very interesting, especially, my favorite character, Bonnet. I especially liked how the author was able to combine ancient occult practices and mix in 21st century technology.<br /><br />You get a lot of book for the little bit of money it cost, and a lot better of a read than most of the more expensive books by well know authors. I had a great time reading The Book of Occult and I hope to see many more great things from Simon W. Clark.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15615323673981571254">An intriguing and almost breathtaking novel!<br/><br/>I’m not really a fan of occult or mystery stories as I love fantasy and more “epic” readings, but as I stumbled upon the cover of this book, something got me. I read the book in one week (yes, it’s pretty long, that’s why the 4 out of 5 stars) but I have to say it “sucked” all my spare time as I didn’t seem to be able to stop reading it. The thing that I loved is it’s variety; from the incredible amount of locations and the many characters, this book i</span>
  <span id="freeText15615323673981571254" style="display:none">An intriguing and almost breathtaking novel!<br /><br />I’m not really a fan of occult or mystery stories as I love fantasy and more “epic” readings, but as I stumbled upon the cover of this book, something got me. After reading it, I must say I went on surfing the web for occultism sites and did some research. I will definitely look for more books on this subject, because it really resonated with me and my interests.<br /><br />Great job Mr. Clark! <div id="review_898820279" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/898820279" />
    <a title="Lizzie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19079233-lizzie"><img alt="Lizzie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1365081439p2/19079233.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/898820279?book_show_action=true">Apr 02, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lizzie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lizzie" href="/user/show/19079233-lizzie">Lizzie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer898820279" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer637789119249134723">Ever since I read The Da Vinci Code, I’ve been hooked on novels about secret societies, occult knowledge, and powerful people in upper echelons of society trying to protect that knowledge and keeping it from the common people. The Book of Occult was a real page-turner in that respect, and didn’t disappoint! Peter loses his childhood friend to a strange ritual they perform as kids and sets out for Paris years later to find out what exactly is in the old manuscript he owns (the one he used to do t</span>
  <span id="freeText637789119249134723" style="display:none">Ever since I read The Da Vinci Code, I’ve been hooked on novels about secret societies, occult knowledge, and powerful people in upper echelons of society trying to protect that knowledge and keeping it from the common people. The Book of Occult was a real page-turner in that respect, and didn’t disappoint! Peter loses his childhood friend to a strange ritual they perform as kids and sets out for Paris years later to find out what exactly is in the old manuscript he owns (the one he used to do the ritual when he was younger). Soon, he is plunged into a whirlwind of adventure involving a secret society trying to use occult knowledge to solve world problems, and while reading, I myself as a reader learned a lot about occult knowledge without feeling bored for a single moment – it was all integrated into the narrative very well. If people think it is far-fetched to assume that occult powers may be at work to control the world, they might think again after reading The Book of Occult. It’s rather skillful how plausible the author makes it seem that something like this might actually be happening. Nothing too much over the top like David Icke, but solid writing and a captivating plot make this book a joy to read. Don’t know if there will be any sequels, but I would very much like to read those too.</span>
  <a data-text-id="637789119249134723" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer915596950" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6101189636911357745">I really enjoyed the smooth writing style of Simon W. Clark in his book "The Book of Occult". I found it to be well written with plenty of fast-paced twists and turns to keep you interested. The story unfolds in a natural way and isn't rushed but at the same time the reader doesn't get bored either. As I said; "well written." Simon did a great job of pulling at the readers emotions and mixing the two main characters story lines until a climatic end.<br/><br/>I found this book to be great fantasy and myste</span>
  <span id="freeText6101189636911357745" style="display:none">I really enjoyed the smooth writing style of Simon W. Clark in his book "The Book of Occult". I found it to be well written with plenty of fast-paced twists and turns to keep you interested. The story unfolds in a natural way and isn't rushed but at the same time the reader doesn't get bored either. As I said; "well written." Simon did a great job of pulling at the readers emotions and mixing the two main characters story lines until a climatic end.<br /><br />I found this book to be great fantasy and mystery reading with a nice blend of occultism, historical fiction, science fiction with present day technology. Wow, what a mix! Anyway, it reminded me of The Da Vinci Code with the characters traveling all over trying to unravel the mysteries of the ancient occult. I love to travel too so that helped draw me into the story-line. The occultism seemed well researched and believable. Although I'm no expert, I didn't catch myself going "yea right??" over and over again as I read.<br /><br />I would recommend this book to anyone who loves a great mystery with their occultism, mixed with just the right amount of geek to keep things interesting. Simon has done a great job in this book with well crafted plots and sub-plots and even some romance that was tastefully and appropriately worked into the story-line. I look forward to reading more of this quality of work from this author. Very well written. I have no problem giving this book 5 stars!</span>
  <a data-text-id="6101189636911357745" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12868995918188285001">As debut novels go, "The Book of the Occult" sets the bar very high for its very talented author, Simon. W. Clark, to top. The reader is swept up into the story of Peter Ashton who, as a teen, attempted to perform an occult ritual that resulted in the death of his best friend. Many years later, Peter sets off to Europe to research the book he used to perform the ritual and finds himself entangled in a web that includes a murderous former government agent, a secret society, gypsies, and things mu</span>
  <span id="freeText12868995918188285001" style="display:none">As debut novels go, "The Book of the Occult" sets the bar very high for its very talented author, Simon. W. Clark, to top. The reader is swept up into the story of Peter Ashton who, as a teen, attempted to perform an occult ritual that resulted in the death of his best friend. Many years later, Peter sets off to Europe to research the book he used to perform the ritual and finds himself entangled in a web that includes a murderous former government agent, a secret society, gypsies, and things much more dark and frightening than he could ever imagine. The plot of this story is rich in detail and filled with well-defined and memorable characters. It never drags and keeps the reader engaged from start to finish. I'm sure you will enjoy this fantastic blend of historical, occult, and suspense fiction as much I did.</span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15770106884330922787">This was a ripping thriller that for me took occult and mystery to the next level. I loved the flow through the story telling and the well crafted plots. The danger that the main character Peter encounters mixed with the original style of the author. Also liked the mix of technology with esoteric theories. <br/>A superb tale that combines real with fantasy in a believable and exciting tale. Couldn't put it down till I was finished so great effort from this author.</span>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

<div id="review_907307092" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/907307092" />
    <a title="H.M. Christi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27229941-h-m-christi"><img alt="H.M. Christi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388650898p2/27229941.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/907307092?book_show_action=true">Apr 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="H.M. Christi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="H.M. Christi" href="/user/show/27229941-h-m-christi">H.M. Christi</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer907307092" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3885215430362611794">The Book of Occult by Simon W. Clark is what I call intense and intelligent writing! The book grabbed a hold of me from start to finish. I found it thrilling, suspenseful, and intellectually stimulating with gripping twists and turns that have you longing for more! Simon W. Clark is a very talented writer with a highly creative imagination that he knows exactly how to convey to the reader, making it easy to visualize and even FEEL the scenes in the book and the lives and personalities of the cha</span>
  <span id="freeText3885215430362611794" style="display:none">The Book of Occult by Simon W. Clark is what I call intense and intelligent writing! The book grabbed a hold of me from start to finish. I found it thrilling, suspenseful, and intellectually stimulating with gripping twists and turns that have you longing for more! Simon W. Clark is a very talented writer with a highly creative imagination that he knows exactly how to convey to the reader, making it easy to visualize and even FEEL the scenes in the book and the lives and personalities of the characters that just come to life as you read the words. I found myself wide-eyed and scrolling through the pages with anxiety and thrill in this seat gripping suspense filled novel, with a wonderfully crafted plot. I look forward to more from this skilled author and I highly recommend this book!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3885215430362611794" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1026699918" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1026699918" />
    <a title="Chris Becker" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7000955-chris-becker"><img alt="Chris Becker" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442611096p2/7000955.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1026699918?book_show_action=true">Aug 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chris Becker" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chris Becker" href="/user/show/7000955-chris-becker">Chris Becker</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1026699918" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17769787321858755726">The Book of Occult is an entertaining tale, well researched and well told. The basic story features a protagonist named Peter Ashton, who, as a teenager, finds an ancient occult text. His friend dies after trying to perform a ritual from the book. Twenty years later, Peter is thrown back into the fray, and races across Europe to try to avert disaster. The basic storyline reminded me of the classic Necronomicon tales of the old master H.P. Lovecraft. But this novel is more modern, like Neal Gaima</span>
  <span id="freeText17769787321858755726" style="display:none">The Book of Occult is an entertaining tale, well researched and well told. The basic story features a protagonist named Peter Ashton, who, as a teenager, finds an ancient occult text. His friend dies after trying to perform a ritual from the book. Twenty years later, Peter is thrown back into the fray, and races across Europe to try to avert disaster. The basic storyline reminded me of the classic Necronomicon tales of the old master H.P. Lovecraft. But this novel is more modern, like Neal Gaiman, Dan Brown, or Dean Koontz.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17769787321858755726" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('3wGzPow7stXxlssF8zVN6bTSKlN7/yXEtP0+tMDwk7zlJ9rsN2V7vVa9f2QEwEc2Yo3Nm7Vyq6Pvg3gFDbNhJg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('S1ySdL8u7mdByDkhL/suYrrpzgxNEvTT5SD4GwT9Q8pxevumBHAnD+bjjUDYDiS9bLYpxIOferS+Xr6qyb6xUA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

  <span id="freeText7925608428776709058" style="display:none">Simon W Clark has been writing all his life. Never formally trained he holds a Commerce Degree in Marketing. His latest novel 'Think Fast or Die' is a spy thriller set in the Middle East. The last published novel he wrote was a supernatural thriller that is now out of print. Simon lives with his family in Melbourne, Australia. He continues to travel whenever possible to unexplored destinations that also provides inspiration for his novels. Otherwise he can be found working his day job in online advertising or relaxing with family and friends.<br /> Further information can be found at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.simonwclark.com">www.simonwclark.com</a>.</span>
